   <h1 id="firstHeading" class="firstHeading" lang="en">List of countries by life expectancy</h1> 
   <div id="bodyContent" class="mw-body-content"> 
    <div id="siteSub" class="noprint">
     From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia
    </div> 
    <div id="contentSub"></div> 
    <div id="contentSub2"></div> 
    <div id="jump-to-nav"></div> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">Jump to search</a> 
    <div id="mw-content-text" lang="en" dir="ltr" class="mw-content-ltr">
     <div class="mw-parser-output">
      <div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">
       Countries by life expectancy at birth
      </div> 
      <p class="mw-empty-elt"> </p> 
      <div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">
       See also: <a href="/wiki/List_of_countries_by_past_life_expectancy" title="List of countries by past life expectancy">List of countries by past life expectancy</a>
      </div> 
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:402px;">
        <a href="/wiki/File:Comparison_gender_life_expectancy_CIA_factbook.svg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Comparison_gender_life_expectancy_CIA_factbook.svg/400px-Comparison_gender_life_expectancy_CIA_factbook.svg.png" decoding="async" width="400" height="350" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Comparison_gender_life_expectancy_CIA_factbook.svg/600px-Comparison_gender_life_expectancy_CIA_factbook.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Comparison_gender_life_expectancy_CIA_factbook.svg/800px-Comparison_gender_life_expectancy_CIA_factbook.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="512" data-file-height="448"></a> 
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a href="/wiki/File:Comparison_gender_life_expectancy_CIA_factbook.svg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a>
         </div>Comparison of average female and male life expectancy as defined in the 2018 CIA Factbook, with selected bubbles labelled. The dotted line corresponds to equal female and male life expectancy. The apparent 3D volumes of the bubbles are linearly proportional to their population.<sup id="cite_ref-iuonoa_1-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-iuonoa-1">[1]</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">[2]</a></sup> (In <a class="external text" href="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/b2/Comparison_gender_life_expectancy_CIA_factbook.svg">the SVG file</a>, hover over a bubble to highlight it and show its data.)
        </div>
       </div>
      </div> 
      <p>The article documents lists of countries by average <a href="/wiki/Life_expectancy" title="Life expectancy">life expectancy</a> at birth by various sources of estimates. </p> 
      <div id="toc" class="toc" role="navigation" aria-labelledby="mw-toc-heading">

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Methodology">Methodology</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_by_life_expectancy&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Methodology">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p>The life expectancy is shown separately for males, and for females, as well as a combined figure. Several non-<a href="/wiki/Sovereign_state" title="Sovereign state">sovereign entities</a> are also included in this list. </p>
      <p>The figures reflect the quality of healthcare in the countries listed as well as other factors including ongoing wars, obesity, and HIV infections. </p>
      <p>Worldwide, the average life expectancy at birth was 71 years (70 years for males and 72 years for females) over the period 2010–2015 according to United Nations World Population Prospects 2015 Revision,<sup id="cite_ref-WPP2010_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WPP2010-3">[3]</a></sup> or 69 years (67 years for males and 71.1 years for females) for 2016 according to <i><a href="/wiki/The_World_Factbook" title="The World Factbook">The World Factbook</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-cia2012_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-cia2012-4">[4]</a></sup> According to the 2015 <a href="/wiki/World_Health_Organization" title="World Health Organization">World Health Organization</a> (WHO) data, women on average live longer than men in all major regions and in all individual countries. </p>
      <p>The countries with the lowest overall life expectancies per the WHO are <a href="/wiki/Sierra_Leone" title="Sierra Leone">Sierra Leone</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Central_African_Republic" title="Central African Republic">Central African Republic</a>, the <a href="/wiki/Democratic_Republic_of_the_Congo" title="Democratic Republic of the Congo">Democratic Republic of the Congo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Guinea-Bissau" title="Guinea-Bissau">Guinea-Bissau</a>, <a href="/wiki/Lesotho" title="Lesotho">Lesotho</a>, <a href="/wiki/Somalia" title="Somalia">Somalia</a>, <a href="/wiki/Eswatini" title="Eswatini">Eswatini</a>, <a href="/wiki/Angola" title="Angola">Angola</a>, <a href="/wiki/Chad" title="Chad">Chad</a>, <a href="/wiki/Mali" title="Mali">Mali</a>, <a href="/wiki/Burundi" title="Burundi">Burundi</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cameroon" title="Cameroon">Cameroon</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Mozambique" title="Mozambique">Mozambique</a>. Of those countries, only Lesotho, Eswatini, and Mozambique in 2011 were suffering from an <a href="/wiki/HIV_prevalence" class="mw-redirect" title="HIV prevalence">HIV prevalence</a> rate of greater than 12 percent in the 15–49 age group.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup> </p>
      <p>Comparing life expectancies from birth across countries can be problematic. There are differing definitions of live birth vs stillbirth even among more developed countries and less developed countries often have poor reporting.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup> </p> 
      <h2><span id="UNDP_.282018.29"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="UNDP_(2018)"><a href="/wiki/UNDP" class="mw-redirect" title="UNDP">UNDP</a> (2018)</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_by_life_expectancy&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: UNDP (2018)">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>

      <h2><span id="List_by_the_United_Nations.2C_for_2010.E2.80.932015"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="List_by_the_United_Nations,_for_2010–2015">List by the United Nations, for 2010–2015</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_by_life_expectancy&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: List by the United Nations, for 2010–2015">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p>On July 2015, the Population Division of the <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Department_of_Economic_and_Social_Affairs" title="United Nations Department of Economic and Social Affairs">United Nations Department of Economic and Social Affairs</a> (UN DESA), released <i>World Population Prospects, The 2015 Revision</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-WPP2010_3-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-WPP2010-3">[3]</a></sup> The following table shows the life expectancy at birth for the period 2010 to 2015. </p>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="List_from_the_GBD_2010_study">List from the GBD 2010 study</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_by_life_expectancy&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: List from the GBD 2010 study">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <p>The Global Burden of Disease 2010 study published updated figures in 2012,<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">[13]</a></sup> including recalculations of life expectancies<sup id="cite_ref-auto_14-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-auto-14">[14]</a></sup> which differ substantially in places from the UN estimates for 2010 (reasons for this are discussed in the freely available appendix to the paper, pages 25–27, currently not available). Although no estimate is given for the sexes combined, for the first time life expectancy estimates have included uncertainty intervals. </p>
      <p><br> </p>

      <h2><span class="mw-headline" id="External_links">External links</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=List_of_countries_by_life_expectancy&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: External links">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2> 
      <ul>
       <li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.helpage.org/global-agewatch/population-ageing-data/">Global Agewatch</a> has the latest internationally comparable statistics on life expectancy from 195 countries.</li> 
       <li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://web.archive.org/web/20110113085832/http://graphs.gapminder.org/world/#$majorMode=chart$is;shi=t;ly=2003;lb=f;il=t;fs=11;al=30;stl=t;st=t;nsl=t;se=t$wst;tts=C$ts;sp=6;ti=2007$zpv;v=0$inc_x;mmid=XCOORDS;iid=phAwcNAVuyj1jiMAkmq1iMg;by=ind$inc_y;mmid=YCOORDS;iid=phAwcNAVuyj2tPLxKvvnNPA;by=ind$inc_s;uniValue=8.21;iid=phAwcNAVuyj0XOoBL_n5tAQ;by=ind$inc_c;uniValue=255;gid=CATID0;by=grp$map_x;scale=log;dataMin=194;dataMax=96846$map_y;scale=lin;dataMin=23;dataMax=86$map_s;sma=49;smi=2.65$cd;bd=0$inds=">Life expectancy trends interactive graph</a></li> 
       <li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.statsilk.com/maps/life-expectancy-interactive-world-map">Life expectancy interactive world map</a></li> 
       <li><a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.livescience.com/22005-highest-and-lowest-life-expectancy-at-birth-infographic.html">Global Life Expectancy (Infographic)|LiveScience</a></li>
